(function (window) {
  function jw() {
    this._functions = [];
    this.run = function (func) {
      this._functions.push(func);
    };
    this.resolve = function (arg) {
      this.run = function (func) {
        func(arg);
      };
      for (var i = 0; i < this._functions.length; i++) {
        var func = this._functions[i];
        delete this._functions[i];
        func(arg);
      }
    };
  }
  var rqw = new jw();

  window.rqw = function (fnc) {
    rqw.run(fnc);
  };
  window.rqw.resolve = function () {
    return rqw.resolve.apply(rqw, arguments);
  };
  var jqw = new jw();
  window.jqw = function (fnc) {
    jqw.run(fnc);
  };
  window.jqw.resolve = function () {
    return jqw.resolve.apply(jqw, arguments);

})(window);

    if (typeof win['page_tag_info']['tags'] == 'undefined') {
      var tags = Drupal.settings.catalog.info.conjunction_term;
      var termParents = Drupal.settings.catalog.info.term_parents;

      if (typeof termParents === 'object') {
        var conjunctionTermParents = [];
        for (var tid in termParents) {
          if (termParents.hasOwnProperty(tid)) {
            conjunctionTermParents = conjunctionTermParents.concat(termParents[tid]);
          }
        }

        if (conjunctionTermParents.length) {
          tags = tags.concat(conjunctionTermParents);
        }
      }

      win['page_tag_info']['tags'] = tags;
    }
  } catch (e) {
  }
  win['banners_inline'] = function (id) {
    try {
      var ob = Drupal.settings.banners_inline.banners[id];
      var curstate;
      if (typeof win.Adapt !== "undefined") {
        curstate = win.Adapt.getCurrentState();
      } else {
        curstate = 'full';
      }
      for (var i = 0; i < ob.length; i++) {
        var block = ob[i];
        if ((typeof block.adapt_states !== "undefined" && block.adapt_states.length > 0 && -1 !== block.adapt_states.indexOf(curstate))
            || ((!block.adapt_states || block.adapt_states.length === 0) && curstate === 'full')) {
          var fallback = (typeof block.fallback !== 'undefined') ? block.fallback : '' 
              classes = (typeof block.classes !== 'undefined') ? block.classes : '' 
              ,pref = '<span class="brocock '+classes+'" data-fallback="'+fallback+'">', suf = '</span>';
          win.document.write(pref+block.code+suf);
          break;
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {
    }
  };
  win['banners_inline_framelistener'] = win['banners_inline_framelistener'] || {};
})(this);

<script>
    var reloadable_banners = {};

    function reload_banners(){
        try{
            if(!document.hidden){
                for (let banner_id in reloadable_banners){
                    let banner_element = document.getElementById(banner_id);
                    if(!!banner_element){
                        let b = banner_element.getBoundingClientRect();
                        if( (b.top+b.height/2)>0 && (b.top+b.height/2)<window.innerHeight){
                            window.reloadable_banners[banner_id] += 1;
                            if(window.reloadable_banners[banner_id]==7){
                                // window.reloadable_banners[banner_id] = 0;
                                banner_element.style.minHeight = b.height+"px";
                                Ya.adfoxCode.reload(banner_id);
                                try{
                                    ym(8092381,'reachGoal','ad_reload',{ 'ad_reload': banner_id });
                                }catch(e){}
                            }
                        }
                    };
                };
            };
            // console.log( reloadable_banners );
        }catch(e){}
    };

    setInterval(reload_banners, 5000);


    function AdFox_banner_create(containerId, banner_params, w, n, lazy=false){
        
            var params = banner_params;
    
            params.p2 = params.p2 || 'hhvm';
            params.pp = params.pp || (w.innerWidth >= 336 ? 'bqzc':'bqzd');
            params.ps = params.ps || 'crea';

            try{var info1 = w.page_tag_info;}catch(e){}
            
            var ad_keys = '';
            try{ad_keys += ' n'+w.Drupal.settings.site.nid;}catch(e){}
            try{ad_keys += ' n'+info1.prod_id;}catch(e){}
            try{ad_keys += ' t'+info1.tags.join(' t');}catch(e){}
            try{ad_keys += ' t'+info1.category_tids.join(' t');}catch(e){}
        
            try{if(!!info1.type_id){ ad_keys += ' t'+info1.type_id;}}catch(e){}
            try{if(!!info1.brand_id){ ad_keys += ' t'+info1.brand_id;}}catch(e){}
        
            try{
                params['pk'] = ad_keys;
                params['pke'] = 1;
            }catch(e){}
        
            try{params['puid1'] = info1.tags.join(':');}catch(e){}
            try{params['puid2'] = info1.prod_id;}catch(e){}
            try{params['puid3'] = w.Drupal.settings.site.type;}catch(e){}
            try{params['puid4'] = Math.floor(Math.random() * 10)}catch(e){}
            try{params['puid5'] = w.Drupal.settings.site.uid != 0 }catch(e){}
            try{params['puid6'] = (info1.gavgav === 'gavgav'+'_0') ? 'no' : 'yes'; }catch(e){}
        
            try{
                params['puid7'] = w.ab_var;
            }catch(e){}
    


            try{
                if((document.cookie.indexOf('kaswo=1')>=0) && (w.Drupal.settings.site.uid==0)){
                    params['puid8'] = 21;
                    params['partner-stat-id'] = 21;
                }
            }catch(e){}
    

            if(lazy){
                w.yaContextCb.push(()=>{
                    Ya.adfoxCode.createScroll({
                        ownerId: 265680,
                        containerId: containerId,
                        params: params,
                        lazyLoad: {
                            fetchMargin: 200,
                            mobileScaling: 2,
                        },
                        onRender: function() { try{ window.reloadable_banners[containerId] = document.getElementById(containerId).classList.contains("NOREFRESH")?-100:0; }catch(e){} }
                    })
                });
            }else{
                w.yaContextCb.push(()=>{
                    Ya.adfoxCode.create({
                        ownerId: 265680,
                        containerId: containerId,
                        params: params,
                        onRender: function() { try{ window.reloadable_banners[containerId] = document.getElementById(containerId).classList.contains("NOREFRESH")?-100:0; }catch(e){} }
                    })
                });
                // console.log(params);
            }
        
    }
        
        
    function ADX_banner_create(containerId, adx_ad_slot, adx_container_style, w, data_ad_client='ca-pub-1304546668536330', auto_responsive=false ){
    
            try {
                if(w.page_tag_info.gavgav === 'gavgav_0'){    
                    // var adx_div_container = w.document.getElementById(containerId);
                    // adx_div_container.innerHTML = '<ins class="adsbygoogle"      style="' + adx_container_style + '"      data-ad-client="ca-pub-8313361070310510"      data-ad-slot="' + adx_ad_slot + '"></ins>';
    
                    var ins   = document.createElement("ins");
                    ins.setAttribute('class','adsbygoogle');
                    ins.setAttribute('style', adx_container_style);
                    ins.setAttribute('data-ad-client', data_ad_client);
                    ins.setAttribute('data-ad-slot', adx_ad_slot);
                    
                    if(auto_responsive){
                        ins.setAttribute('data-ad-format','auto');
                        ins.setAttribute('data-full-width-responsive','true');
                    }
    
                    w.document.getElementById(containerId).appendChild(ins);                
    
                    (w.adsbygoogle = w.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
                }
            } catch (e) {};
        
    }

<script>

function botbot_check () {
    try{
        var raw = navigator.userAgent.match(/Chrom(e|ium)\/([0-9]+)\./);
        const chrome = raw ? parseInt(raw[2], 10) : false;
        const old_chrome = chrome>0 && chrome<89;

        var raw = navigator.userAgent.match(/Firefox\/([0-9]+)\./);
        const ff = raw ? parseInt(raw[1], 10) : false;
        const old_ff = ff>0 && ff<60;

        const wd_ok = (window.navigator.webdriver===false) || ((old_chrome || old_ff) && (window.navigator.webdriver!==true));
        const wd_fake = !!Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor(window.navigator, 'webdriver');

        const is_bot = ( !wd_ok || wd_fake );

        return is_bot;

    }catch(e){};
};

try{
    window.botbot = botbot_check();
    // ym(8092381,'params',{'botbot':window.botbot});
}catch(e){};

</script>

<script>
rqw(function (r) {
    r(["https://openfpcdn.io/botd/v1/iife.min.js"], 
    function (m) {
        try{
            var botdPromise = BotD.load({ monitoring: false })

            botdPromise
                .then((botd) => botd.detect())
                .then((result) => botd2ym(result))
                .catch((error) => ym(8092381,'params',{'botd7':'err_detecting'}))
        }catch(e){}
    }, 
    function (e){
        ym(8092381,'params',{'botd7':{'err_loading':''+runBotDetection()}})
    });
});


function botd2ym(r){
    let botname = r.bot?r.botKind:'humanoid'; 
    let params = {'botd7':{}};
    params['botd7'][botname] = ''+runBotDetection();
    try{ym(8092381,'params',params);}catch(e){};
    // console.log( params );
}

runBotDetection = function () {
    try{
        var raw = navigator.userAgent.match(/Chrom(e|ium)\/([0-9]+)\./);
        const chrome = raw ? parseInt(raw[2], 10) : false;
        const old_chrome = chrome>0 && chrome<89;

        var raw = navigator.userAgent.match(/Firefox\/([0-9]+)\./);
        const ff = raw ? parseInt(raw[1], 10) : false;
        const old_ff = ff>0 && ff<60;

        const fake_old_chrome = !!navigator.userAgentData && old_chrome;
        const fake_old_ff = !!navigator.credentials && old_ff;


        let chromium = false;
        try{ chromium = navigator.userAgentData.brands.find(x=>x.brand=='Chromium').version; }catch(e){ }

        // const old = !navigator.userAgentData;
        const wd_ok = (window.navigator.webdriver===false) || (old_chrome && (window.navigator.webdriver!==true) );
        const wd_nfake = !!Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor(window.navigator, 'webdriver');

        let wd_pfake = 'XZ';
        let d = Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor(Navigator.prototype, 'webdriver');
        try{ wd_pfake = (((typeof d) == "undefined") || !d.get || (d.get.toString().indexOf('webdriver')===-1) ); }catch(e){};

        let uafake = 'XZ';
        let ua = Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor(Navigator.prototype, 'userAgent');
        try{ uafake = (((typeof ua) == "undefined") || !ua.get || (ua.get.toString().indexOf('userAgent')===-1) ); }catch(e){};

        const is_bot = ( !wd_ok || wd_nfake || fake_old_chrome || fake_old_ff);

        let wd = 'webdriver_'+window.navigator.webdriver
                +' nfake_'+wd_nfake
                +' pfake_'+wd_pfake
                +' twd_'+(typeof navigator.webdriver) 
                +' tpwd_'+(typeof d)
                +' uafake_'+uafake
                // +' tua_'+(typeof navigator.userAgent) 
                // +' tpua_'+(typeof ua)
                +' old_'+(old_chrome||old_ff)
                +' cr_'+chrome
                +' crmm_'+chromium
                +' cce_'+(chrome==chromium)
                +' ccl_'+(chrome<chromium)
                +' foc_'+fake_old_chrome
                +' ff_'+ff
                +' fof_'+fake_old_ff
                +' bot_'+is_bot
                +' botbot_'+window.botbot
                ;
        return wd;
    }catch(e){};
};


</script>
